					<h2 id="mainHeading">Site Moved</h2>
					
					<p>The Group 1 Software website has been discontinued and has been replaced by the Pitney Bowes Software website. 
						For support of your Group 1 Software product, visit <a href="http://www.g1.com/Support/" title="Group 1 Support website">http://www.g1.com/Support/</a>. 
						For information about our products, please visit <a href="http://www.pb.com/software" title="Pitney Bowes Software website">http://www.pb.com/software</a>.</p>

	<div class="main" role="main" data-hires="true">
		<header class="section section-hero">
			<div class="section-content">
				<h1 class="center-text">Turn wherever you are into your very own screening room.</h1>
				<p>iTunes makes it easy to lose yourself in a movie or TV show, whether you’re relaxing at home or out in the world. Just download your favorite episodes or movies and you have something great to watch while you’re commuting to work, traveling, or just standing in line somewhere. You can enjoy bonus movie content like deleted and alternate scenes with iTunes Extras. And if you can’t decide what to watch, check out Top TV Seasons or the handpicked Movie of the Week.</p>
				<figure class="hero-hero">
					<p class="image-caption"><a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/movie/captain-fantastic/id1127934488" class="icon icon-external no-oldie"><strong><em>Captain Fantastic</em></strong> is available on iTunes</a></p>
				</figure>
			</div>
		</header>

		<section class="section section-tap-away">
			<div class="section-content">
				<h2 class="center-text">All your movies and TV shows are just a tap away.</h2>
				<p class="hero-text">Whatever you feel like watching — a Hollywood blockbuster, a hit TV series, or a  documentary — iTunes keeps your entire collection of movies and TV shows organized and ready to play. So you can easily browse your library for something great to watch. Or find something entirely new on the iTunes Store.<sup>1</sup></p>
				<figure>
					<div class="tap-away-hero"></div>
					<p class="image-caption"><a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/movie/finding-dory/id1122228373" class="icon icon-external no-oldie"><strong><em>Finding Dory</em></strong> is available on iTunes</a></p>
					<figcaption class="caption">
						<ul class="device-options row">
							<li class="ios column large-4">
								<figure class="ios-tv-hero"></figure>
								<div class="text">
									<h4>On iPhone, iPad, and iPod touch.</h4>
									<p>Open the TV app to see your movies and TV shows and content from HBO NOW, Hulu, and more.</p>
								</div>
							</li>
							<li class="osx column large-4">
								<figure class="osx-music-hero"></figure>
								<div class="text">
									<h4>On Mac and PC.</h4>
									<p>Open iTunes, go to Library, and select Movies or TV Shows.</p>
								</div>
							</li>
							<li class="appletv column large-4">
								<figure class="appletv-music-hero-us"></figure>
								<div class="text">
									<h4>On Apple TV.</h4>
									<p>Select Movies, TV Shows, or the TV app from the Home screen.</p>
								</div>
							</li>
						</ul>
					</figcaption>
				</figure>
			</div>
		</section>

		<section class="section section-extras">
			<div class="section-content">
				<div class="text column large-6">
					<h2 class="has-violator">iTunes Extras</h2>
					<p>iTunes Extras adds even more to your movie-watching experience. Purchase select HD movies and you’ll get bonus content like behind-the-scenes footage, cast and crew interviews, even deleted and alternate scenes.<sup>2</sup></p>
				</div>
				<figure class="extras-hero column large-6">
					<p class="image-caption"><a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/movie/ghostbusters-2016/id1125586234" class="icon icon-external no-oldie"><strong><em>Ghostbusters</em></strong> is available on iTunes</a></p>
				</figure>
			</div>
		</section>

		<section class="section section-store">
			<div class="section-content">
				<h2 class="center-text">iTunes Store.</h2>
				<h2 class="subheadline center-text">Go from media lover to media mogul.</h2>
				<p>The iTunes Store is the place to get all your video entertainment. There are over 85,000 movies you can buy or rent<sup>3</sup> — including blockbusters, indies, and classics. And with more than 300,000 commercial-free TV shows,<sup>3</sup> you’re sure to find a series to keep you hooked.</p>
			</div>
		</section>

		<section class="section section-movies">
			<div class="section-content">
				<div class="text column large-6">
					<h2>Movies.</h2>
					<h2 class="subheadline">Now showing on all your screens.</h2>
					<p>Browse more than 85,000 comedies, romances, classics, indies, and thrillers. iTunes has movies from every major Hollywood studio and independents around the world. And you can buy or rent them in 1080p HD. Purchase on your iOS device, and your movie will be instantly accessible in your iTunes library on your Mac or PC. And vice versa. Tap to play, or download to keep a copy with you when you won’t have Wi-Fi. You can also watch on your HDTV via Apple TV.</p>
				</div>

				<figure class="movies-hero column large-6"></figure>
			</div>
		</section>

		<section class="section section-tv-shows">
			<div class="section-content">
				<figure class="tv-shows-hero column large-6"></figure>

				<div class="text column large-6">
					<h2>TV Shows.</h2>
					<h2 class="subheadline">Take your shows on the road.</h2>
					<p>iTunes brings you over 300,000 TV shows commercial-free — many in HD. Buy individual episodes or a full season. With Season Pass, you can prepay for a full season and download episodes as they become available. And with Complete My Season, you can buy an episode or two to check out a show, then get the whole season for the original price minus what you’ve already paid. Whether you buy on your Mac, PC, Apple TV, or iOS device, TV shows are instantly accessible in your iTunes library.</p>
				</div>
			</div>
		</section>

		<section class="section section-family-sharing">
			<div class="section-content center-text">
				<h2 class="has-violator">Family Sharing.</h2>
				<h2 class="subheadline center-text">Share all your content. And maybe your popcorn.</h2>
				<p>Family Sharing makes it easy for up to six people in your family to share each other’s iTunes purchases. Whenever one person buys a new movie or TV show, everybody in your family can download and enjoy it. Families can share songs and albums, too. And for kids under age 13, or any other family members you choose, you can turn on Ask to Buy, which requires parental permission before purchasing.<sup>4</sup></p>
				<a href="/ios/whats-new/family-sharing/" class="more">Learn more</a>
				<figure>
					<div class="family-sharing-hero"></div>
					<figcaption class="row caption">
						<p class="column large-4 invite">Set up Family Sharing for up to six people.</p>
						<p class="column large-4 share">Family members can download what they want with a tap.</p>
						<p class="column large-4 control">Have kids ask permission before making purchases.</p>
					</figcaption>
				</figure>
			</div>
		</section>

		<section class="section section-everywhere">
			<div class="section-content">
				<h2 class="center-text">Buy once, available everywhere.</h2>
				<p>With iCloud, the movies and TV shows you buy from the iTunes Store automatically appear on all your devices.<sup>5</sup> Movies and TV shows purchased on any device are instantly accessible in your iTunes library on your Mac, PC, or Apple TV.<sup>5</sup> Just tap to play, or even download if you’re going somewhere you won’t have Wi-Fi. If you start watching a movie and stop before the end, iCloud remembers where you left off. So you can pick up in the same spot on any of your devices. And with Family Sharing, whenever one person buys a new movie or TV show, everybody gets to watch.</p>
				<figure class="everywhere-hero"></figure>
			</div>
		</section>

		<section class="section section-gifts f-16">
			<div class="section-content">
				<figure class="gifts-hero column large-12 fall-16"></figure>
				<div class="text column large-12">
					<h2>Gift Cards</h2>
					<p>Send friends and family an iTunes Gift Card or Apple Music Gift Card from your iOS device or computer.<sup>6</sup> You can buy gift cards in a range of denominations, and recipients can choose whatever they want, including an Apple Music membership, or anything from the iTunes Store,<sup>1</sup> App Store, iBooks Store, and Mac App Store.</p>
					<ul>
						<li><a href="/itunes/gifts/" class="more">Learn more</a></li>
						<li>Already have an iTunes or Apple Music Gift Card? <a href="https://buy.itunes.apple.com/WebObjects/MZFinance.woa/wa/redeemLandingPage" class="more">Redeem</a></li>
					</ul>
				</div>
			</div>
		</section>

		<section class="section section-social fall-16">
	<div class="section-content row">

<script>
	function appendGallery() {

		if ( $('body').hasClass('append-gallery') ) {
			$('#posts').children('.jq:visible').children('article:last').after( $('#posts').children('article') );
		}

		$('ul.social-icons-list li a.btn-more-mobile').remove();
		$('.pop-share').append('<a href="javascript:void(0)" class="btn-more-mobile icon-more" title="Mais"></a>');

    	$('.info-share-new .btn-close, .overlay-share-new').on('click', function(e){
            e.preventDefault();
		    $('.overlay-share-new').fadeOut();
		    $('.info-share-new').fadeOut();

        });

		$('article .bottom-info').on('click', '.btn-more-mobile', function(e){
		    e.preventDefault();
		    var inputDados = $(this).parents('.bottom-info').find('.urlInput');
		    //recolher o título, link do post e copiar o link do input hidden
		    var title_share = inputDados.attr( "name" ),
	            texto_share = inputDados.attr( "placeholder" ),
	            url_share = inputDados.attr( "value" ),
		        hrefWA = "whatsapp://send?text=" + texto_share,
		        hrefDq = url_share + "#comentarios",
		        texto_mailto = "mailto:destinatario@email.com.br?&body=" + encodeURI(texto_share),
		        hrefORonclick = '';

		    //facebook -> url_share
		    if($(window).width() <= 320){
		        var hrefORonclick = 'href',
			        hrefFb = "https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=" + url_share,
			        hrefTw = "http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?source=webclient&text="+ texto_share,
			        hrefGp = "https://plus.google.com/share?url=" + url_share,
			        hrefLk = "http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&url=" + url_share;
		    } else{
		        var hrefORonclick = 'onclick';
			        hrefFb = "window.open('https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=" + url_share + "', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');",
			        hrefTw = "window.open('http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?source=webclient&text="+ texto_share +"', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');",
			        hrefGp = "window.open('https://plus.google.com/share?url=" + url_share + "', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');",
			        hrefLk = "window.open('http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&url=" + url_share + "', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');";
		    }

		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.facebook a').attr( hrefORonclick, hrefFb);
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.twitter a').attr( hrefORonclick, hrefTw);
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.google-plus a').attr( hrefORonclick, hrefGp);
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.linkedin a').attr('onclick', hrefLk);
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.whatsapp a').attr('href', hrefWA);
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.btn-comments a').attr('href', hrefDq);
		    //email -> texto_email
		    $('.info-share-new .share-list li.email a').attr('href', texto_mailto);
		    //show overlay & share
		    $('.overlay-share-new').fadeIn();
		    $('.info-share-new').fadeIn();

		});

        $('article').each(function() {
        	console.log('nav');
            var self = $(this),
                selectorInput = $(this).find('.urlInput').val(),
                o = $(this).find('.facebook-count'),
                // c = $(this).find('.twitter-count'),
                e = $(this).find('.google-count');
        	console.log(selectorInput);
        	console.log('-----');
            $.getJSON( 'http://graph.facebook.com/?id=' + selectorInput, function( fbdata ) {
                o.text(fbdata.share.share_count);
            });
            // $.getJSON( 'http://cdn.api.twitter.com/1/urls/count.json?url=' + selectorInput + '&callback=?', function( twitdata ) {

            $.ajax({
    		  type: 'POST',
    		  url: 'https://clients6.google.com/rpc',
    		  processData: true,
    		  contentType: 'application/json',
    		  data: JSON.stringify({
    		    'method':'pos.plusones.get',
    		        'id':'p',
    		        'params':{
    		            'nolog':true,
    		            'id':selectorInput,
    		            'source':'widget',
    		            'userId':'@viewer',
    		            'groupId':'@self'
    		            },
    		        'jsonrpc':'2.0',
    		        'key':'p',
    		        'apiVersion':'v1'
    		  }),
    		  success: function(response) {
    		    e.text(response.result.metadata.globalCounts.count);
    		  }
    		});

			if ( $('a.disqus-comment-count') ) {

				     $('a.disqus-comment-count').each(function() {

	}

					<label for="email">Insira seu e-mail</label>

		<div class="newsletter-box-feedback open" aria-hidden="true" role="presentation" style="display:none">
			<p>Quase no final... Precisamos confirmar o seu endereço de e-mail. <br>Para concluir o processo de assinatura, clique no link existente no e-mail que <br>acabamos de enviar para você.</p>
			<p>Email <em class="form-email">email@email.com</em> já cadastrado. Para atualizar o cadastro, <a href="javascript:void(0)" target="_blank" class="link-cadastro" title="clique aqui">clique aqui</a></p>
		</div><!-- newsletter-box -->


		<script>
			$(function() {
				$('form#newsletter-form').submit(function(e) {
					e.preventDefault();
					var email = $('input#email').val(),
						nome = $('input#nome').val(),
						filtro = /^([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*)@((?:[\w-]+\.)*\w[\w-]{0,66})\.([a-z]{2,6}(?:\.[a-z]{2})?)$/i;;

					var self = $(this);
					var url = self.attr('action');

					self.find('.btn-submit').addClass('off').prop("disabled", true);

					if (email != "" || nome != "") {
						if (filtro.test(email)) {

							$.post(url, self.serialize(), function(data) {

								if ( data === 'sucesso' ) {
									$(".newsletter-box-feedback").children('p:last').hide();
									$(".newsletter-box").hide();
									$(".newsletter-box-feedback").fadeIn();
									self[0].reset();
								} else {
									var dataJson = JSON.parse(data),
										dataCodigo = dataJson.codigo,
										dataMSG = dataJson.msg;

									if ( dataCodigo === 214 ) {
										var link1 = dataMSG.match(/http[s]?:\/\/[a-zA-Z0-9]{1,}.*"/);
										var link = link1[0].replace('"', '');
										$(".newsletter-box-feedback").children('p:first').hide();
										$(".newsletter-box-feedback").children('p:last').find('.form-email').html(email);
										$(".newsletter-box-feedback").children('p:last').find('.link-cadastro').attr('href', link);
										$(".newsletter-box").hide();
										$(".newsletter-box-feedback").fadeIn();
									} else {
										alert( 'Erro '+dataCodigo+' ao cadastrar o e-mail' );
									}

								}
								self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
							});

						} else {
							$("#email").val("Este endereço de email não é válido!");
							self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
							return false;
						} // if regex email
					} else { // if email || nome
						$("#email").val('Digite um email!');
						self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
						return false;
					}
				});
			})
	</script>

<script>
    $('article').each(function() {
        var self = $(this),
            selectorInput = $(this).find('.urlInput').val(),
            o = $(this).find('.facebook-count'),
            // c = $(this).find('.twitter-count'),
            e = $(this).find('.google-count');
        $.getJSON( 'http://graph.facebook.com/?id=' + selectorInput, function( fbdata ) {
            o.text(fbdata.share.share_count);
        }),
        // $.getJSON( 'http://cdn.api.twitter.com/1/urls/count.json?url=' + selectorInput + '&callback=?', function( twitdata ) {
        //     c.text(twitdata.count);
        // });
        $.ajax({
		  type: 'POST',
		  url: 'https://clients6.google.com/rpc',
		  processData: true,
		  contentType: 'application/json',
		  data: JSON.stringify({
		    'method':'pos.plusones.get',
		        'id':'p',
		        'params':{
		            'nolog':true,
		            'id':selectorInput,
		            'source':'widget',
		            'userId':'@viewer',
		            'groupId':'@self'
		            },
		        'jsonrpc':'2.0',
		        'key':'p',
		        'apiVersion':'v1'
		  }),
		  success: function(response) {
		    e.text(response.result.metadata.globalCounts.count);
		  }
		});
    })
</script>

<script>
	$(function() {
		$('a.btn-change-src').click(function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();

			var self = $(this),
				src = self.children('img').attr('src'),
				href = self.attr('href'),
				hrefFb = "window.open('https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=" + href + "', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');",
				hrefTw = "window.open('http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?source=webclient&text=FonteaJorrar: "+ href +"', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');",
				hrefGp = "window.open('https://plus.google.com/share?url=" + href + "', '_blank', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=548,height=325');";

			$('div.lightbox a.icon-facebook').parent().attr('onclick', hrefFb);
			$('div.lightbox a.icon-twitter').parent().attr('onclick', hrefTw);
			$('div.lightbox a.icon-google-plus').parent().attr('onclick', hrefGp);
			$('div.overlay img.lightbox-img').attr('src', src);

			$('header').addClass('fix-zindex');

			$('body > div.box > div.overlay').eq(0).fadeIn(400);
			$('body > div.box > div.overlay').removeClass('zoomin')
		});

		$('.overlay .lightbox').on('click', 'a.btn-close', function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			$('div.overlay').fadeOut(300);
			$('div.overlay').addClass('zoomin');
			$('header').removeClass('fix-zindex');
		});

		$('.btn-share-img-mobile').on('click', function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			$(this).parents('.share-img').next().fadeIn();
			$(this).parents('.share-img').next().next().fadeIn();
		});
	});
</script>

<script>
    $(function() {
        $('form#newsletter-form-modal').submit(function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var email = $('input#email-modal').val(),
                nome = $('input#nome-modal').val(),
                filtro = /^([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*)@((?:[\w-]+\.)*\w[\w-]{0,66})\.([a-z]{2,6}(?:\.[a-z]{2})?)$/i;;

            var self = $(this);
            var url = self.attr('action');

            self.find('.btn-submit').addClass('off').prop("disabled", true);

            if (email != "" || nome != "") {
                if (filtro.test(email)) {

                    $.post(url, self.serialize(), function(data) {

                        if ( data === 'sucesso' ) {
                            $(".newsletter-feedback-modal").children('p:last').hide().parent().slideDown('fast');
                            self[0].reset();
                        } else {
                            var dataJson = JSON.parse(data),
                                dataCodigo = dataJson.codigo,
                                dataMSG = dataJson.msg;

                            if ( dataCodigo === 214 ) {
                                $(".newsletter-feedback-modal").children('p:first').hide().parent().slideDown('fast');
                            } else {
                                alert( 'Erro '+dataCodigo+' ao cadastrar o e-mail' );
                            }
                        }
                        self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
                    });

                } else {
                    $("#email-modal").val("Este endereço de email não é válido!");
                    self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
                    return false;
                } // if regex email
            } else { // if email || nome
                $("#email-modal").val('Digite um email!');
                self.find('.btn-submit').removeClass('off').prop("disabled", false);
                return false;
            }
        });

    })
</script>
